:in range and :out of range css pseudo classes	A										<section class="prog__container"><p>If a temporal or number `<input>` has `max` and/or `min` attributes, then `:in-range` matches when the value is within the specified range and `:out-of-range` matches when the value is outside the specified range. If there are no range constraints, then neither pseudo-class matches.</p><br>IE 11 &#10007;<br>Firefox 50+ &#10003;<br>Chrome 53+ &#10003;<br>Safari TP+ &#10003;<br>iOS Safari 5.0-5.1+ partial<br>Android Browser 53+ &#10003;<p><b>Notes:</b> <p>Note that <code>&lt;input type="range"&gt;</code> can never match <code>:out-of-range</code> because the user cannot input such a value, and if the initial value is outside the range, the browser immediately clamps it to the minimum or maximum (as appropriate) bound of the range.</p></p></section>	http://caniuse.com/css-in-out-of-range
